#ADDED DYNASTIES

##IF A COA DOESN'T WORK - Check capitalization as apparently that matters. house_Artois for example won't work if it's house_artois in the dynasty file
	#If all else fails put the dynasty in the landed_titles file or vise versa. For example the barcelona dynasty is there since it just wouldn't work in this file

#NEW COAS#

#Goal is to remove most my custom .dds files but not all of them will be

#CoA's are a mix from multiple mods since everyone does different titles and in some cases I personally feel a mod did a title better than another that does the same title and then there's also my added titles. Better European Coats of Arms is used for dynamic CoA's
